3. Jen flips the coin. Since "flip" means "reverse," the coin is now tails up.
4. Giselle flips the coin. Again, the coin is reversed, so it is now heads up.
5. Noel does not flip the coin, so it remains heads up.

Therefore, after all the actions, the coin is still heads up.

Based on this sequence of flips, the coin ends up heads up again.
Therefore, the answer (Yes or No) isYes, the coin is still heads up.
